// EXTENT SYS001,WRK14A,1,1,600,300
// DLBL IJSYS02,'DOS.WORKFILE.002',0,SD
// EXTENT SYS002,WRK14A,1,1,900,300
// DLBL IJSYS03,'DOS.WORKFILE.003',0,SD
// EXTENT SYS003,WRK14A,1,1,1200,300
// DLBL IJSYSLN,'DOS.WORKFILE.LNK',0,SD
// EXTENT SYSLNK,WRK14A,1,1,1500,300
// DLBL IJSYSSL,'DOS.SYSRES.FILE.VOLUME.2',,SD
// EXTENT SYSSLB,RES11B,1,1,330,1650
// ASSGN SYS001,X'192'
// ASSGN SYS002,X'192'
// ASSGN SYS003,X'192'
// ASSGN SYSLNK,X'192'
// ASSGN SYSSLB,X'131'   RES11B PRV SLB
// OPTION LINK,NODECK,XREF,DUMP
* ASSEMBLE AND LINK CVT11RES
// EXEC ASSEMBLY

  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                          DOS CL3-10 03/29/70

                                     41 *********************************************************************** C1R00620
                                     42 *                                                                       C1R00630
                                     43 * Create a 199-Cylinder SYSRES on a 2314 disk volume                    C1R00640
                                     44 *    * Matches CORGZ " NEWVOL CL=55(10),RL=77(10),SL=65(10)"            C1R00650
                                     45 *    * Core image directory starts on cyl 0 track 10 for 10 tracks      C1R00660
                                     46 *    * Relocatable and Source Statement directories are 10 tracks each  C1R00670
                                     47 *                                                                       C1R00680
                                     48 *  1. Copy / update as needed library control records to 2314           C1R00690
                                     49 *     a. Cyl 0 Head 1 Record 1: Core image status                       C1R00700
                                     50 *     b. Cyl 0 Head 1 Record 2: pointer to relocatable directory        C1R00710
                                     51 *     c. Cyl 0 Head 1 Record 3: pointer to soure book directory         C1R00720
                                     52 *     d. Cyl 0 Head 1 Record 4: not used (DOS/VS used this for proclib) C1R00730
                                     53 *  3. Copy $$A$IPL2 to 2314 (Cyl 0 Head 1 Record 5)                     C1R00740
                                     54 *  4. Copy Core image library contents from 2311 to 2314                C1R00750
                                     55 *     a. Re-block each phase to reflect 2314 shorter CIL block size     C1R00760
                                     56 *     b. Update directory entry for new placement and block count       C1R00770
                                     57 *     c. Format the balance of the core image directory with empty      C1R00780
                                     58 *        directory records.                                             C1R00790
                                     59 *     d. Format the balance of the core image library with empty        C1R00800
                                     60 *        library records.                                               C1R00810
                                     61 *  5. Copy relocatable module library contents from 2311 to 2314        C1R00820
                                     62 *     a. No reblocking; library blocksizes same on 2311 & 2314          C1R00830
                                     63 *     b. Update directory entry for new placement and block count       C1R00840
                                     64 *     c. Format the balance of the relocatable directory with empty     C1R00850
                                     65 *        directory records.                                             C1R00860
                                     66 *     d. No need to format the balance of the library.  Apparently      C1R00870
                                     67 *        MAINT and CORGZ always use formatting writes when adding       C1R00880
                                     68 *        items to the relocatable library                               C1R00890
                                     69 *  6. Copy source statement library contents from 2311 to 2314          C1R00900
                                     70 *     a. No reblocking; library blocksizes same on 2311 & 2314          C1R00910
                                     71 *     b. Update directory entry for new placement and block count       C1R00920
                                     72 *     c. Format the balance of the relocatable directory with empty     C1R00930
                                     73 *        directory records.                                             C1R00940
                                     74 *     d. No need to format the balance of the library.  Apparently      C1R00950
                                     75 *        MAINT and CORGZ always use formatting writes when adding       C1R00960
                                     76 *        items to the source statement library                          C1R00970
                                     77 *  7. Format/load Cyl 0 Head 5 through Head 9.  These are special       C1R00980
                                     78 *     core image directories for:                                       C1R00990
                                     79 *     a.  $$ transients other than $$BO transients (head 5)             C1R01000
                                     80 *     b.  $$BO open transients (head 6)                                 C1R01010
                                     81 *     c.  $ phases (not including $$ nor $$BO transients) head 7        C1R01020
                                     82 *     d.  FGP..... phases (mostly POWER II phases) (head 8)             C1R01030
                                     83 *     e.  Currently executing phase (head 9)                            C1R01040
                                     84 *  8. Copy IPL bootstrap records from C0H0R1-2 from 2311 to 2314        C1R01050
                                     85 *                                                                       C1R01060
                                     86 *  This program runs in an emulated environment, so no disk error       C1R01070
                                     87 *     checking is needed, nor is it performed.                          C1R01080
                                     88 *                                                                       C1R01090
                                     89 *  And although the Hercules emulator supports the 370 instruction      C1R01100
                                     90 *  set, this program limits itself to S/360 instructions.  Reasons:     C1R01110
                                     91 *                                                                       C1R01120
       CONVERT 2311 SYSRES TO 2314                                                                             PAGE    3


  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                          DOS CL3-10 03/29/70

                                     92 *  1. DOS/360 didn't support the 370 instructions.  A program check     C1R01130
                                     93 *     on a 370 instruction could very well confuse the error handler.   C1R01140
                                     94 *  2. This was the toolset available to assembly-language programmers   C1R01150
                                     95 *     on 360 hardware.  This program serves as an example of how        C1R01160
                                     96 *     things were done 'back in the day.'                               C1R01170
                                     97 *  3. Should there arise another emulator that enforces a S/360         C1R01180
                                     98 *     instruction set, this program will be ready to go.                C1R01190
                                     99 *                                                                       C1R01200
                                    100 *  Even though ICM, STCM, and MVCL would be immensely useful here.      C1R01210
                                    101 *                                                                       C1R01220
                                    102 *********************************************************************** C1R01230

                                    210 *********************************************************************** C1R02310
                                    211 *                                                                       C1R02320
                                    212 * FOR SYSRES, LIBRARIES ALWAYS START ON A CYLINDER BOUNDARY.            C1R02330
                                    213 *                                                                       C1R02340
                                    214 * THE CORE IMAGE LIBRARY ALWAYS STARTS ON CYLINDER ZERO, FOLLOWED BY    C1R02350
                                    215 * THE RELOCATABLE LIBRARY (IF PRESENT) AND THEN THE SOURCE STATEMENT    C1R02360
                                    216 * LIBRARY (IF PRESENT).  A CYLINDER IS RESERVED AT THE END OF SYSRES    C1R02370
                                    217 * FOR STORAGE OF SYSTEM (GLOBAL) AND PARTITION-SPECIFIC JCL.            C1R02380
                                    218 *                                                                       C1R02390
                                    219 * THE FIRST 10 TRACKS OF THE CORE IMAGE LIBRARY ARE USED FOR SYSTEM     C1R02400
                                    220 * PURPOSES, AND THE CORE IMAGE DIRECTORY STARTS TRACK ON 10.  LIBRARY   C1R02410
                                    221 * CONTENT STARTS ON THE FIRST TRACK FOLLOWING THE CORE IMAGE DIRECTORY. C1R02420
                                    222 *                                                                       C1R02430
                                    223 * THE RELOCATABLE LIBRARY STARTS ON THE FIRST CYLINDER FOLLOWING THE    C1R02440
                                    224 * CORE IMAGE LIBRARY. THE DIRECTORY STARTS ON THE FIRST TRACK OF THAT   C1R02450
                                    225 * CYLINDER, AND LIBRARY CONTENT STARTS ON THE FIRST TRACK FOLLOWING     C1R02460
                                    226 * THE DIRECTORY.                                                        C1R02470
                                    227 *                                                                       C1R02480
                                    228 * THE SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY HAS THE SAME LAYOUT AS THE RELOCATABLE   C1R02490
                                    229 * LIBRARY.                                                              C1R02500
                                    230 *                                                                       C1R02510
                                    231 * PRIVATE LIBRARIES HAVE THE SAME LAYOUT AS THE CORRESPONDING SYSTEM    C1R02520
                                    232 * LIBRARY STORED ON SYSRES, INCLUDING TEN TRACKS FOR SYSTEM PURPOSES    C1R02530
                                    233 * AT THE BEGINNING OF THE CORE IMAGE LIBRARY.                           C1R02540
                                    234 *                                                                       C1R02550
                                    235 *********************************************************************** C1R02560



                                    237 *********************************************************************** C1R02580
                                    238 *                                                                       C1R02590
                                    239 * DEFINITIONS FOR THE NEW SYSRES TO BE BUILT ON 2314 DISK               C1R02600
                                    240 *                                                                       C1R02610
                                    241 *********************************************************************** C1R02620

000038                              243 R14CILCL EQU   56                  CORE IMAGE LIB CYLS, INCLUDING CYL 0 C1R02640
00000A                              244 R14CIDTK EQU   10                  CORE IMAGE DIR TRACKS, STARTS C0H10  C1R02650
                                    245 *                                  ...10 IS MIN & MAX ELSE CODE BREAKS  C1R02660
001180                              246 R14CILTB EQU   R14CILCL*G14TKCYL*G14CILBT   CIL LIBRARY BLOCKS TOTAL    C1R02670
                                    247 *                                                                       C1R02680
000038                              248 R14RLBST EQU   R14CILCL            STARTING CYLINDER OF RELO DIR/LIB    C1R02690
00004D                              249 R14RLBCL EQU   77                  RES RELO LIBRARY CYLS                C1R02700
00000A                              250 R14RLDTK EQU   10                  RES RELO DIRECTORY TRACKS            C1R02710
005FA0                              251 R14RLBTB EQU   (R14RLBCL*G14TKCYL-R14RLDTK)*G14RLBBT  RLB TOTAL BLOCKS  C1R02720

       CONVERT 2311 SYSRES TO 2314    DISK READ/WRITE CURSOR                                                   PAGE    9


  LOC  OBJECT CODE    ADDR1 ADDR2  STMT   SOURCE STATEMENT                                          DOS CL3-10 03/29/70

                                    265 *********************************************************************** C1R02860
                                    266 *                                                                       C1R02870
                                    267 *  DISK READ/WRITE CURSOR LAYOUT                                        C1R02880
                                    268 *                                                                       C1R02890
                                    269 *  INCLUDES CURRENT SEEK ADDRESS, ADDRESS OF DTFPH FOR I/O OPERATIONS,  C1R02900
                                    270 *  TRACK GEOMETRY, AND EXTENT INFORMATION FOR DIRECTORY OR LIBRARY      C1R02910
                                    271 *  CURRENTLY POINTED TO BY THE CURSOR.                                  C1R02920
                                    272 *                                                                       C1R02930
                                    273 *  USED TO PASS INFORMATION TO THE FOLLOWING ROUTINES                   C1R02940
                                    274 *                                                                       C1R02950
                                    275 *  XIO -      EXECUTE THE READ OR WRITE OPERATION AT THE BBCCHHR        C1R02960

                                    324 * CORE IMAGE STATUS RECORD IS CYL 0 HEAD 1 REC 1 OF SYSRES FOR A        C1R03450
                                    325 *   SYSTEM CORE IMAGE LIBRARY, AND CYL 0 HEAD 0 REC 1 OF A PRIVATE      C1R03460
                                    326 *   CORE IMAGE LIBRARY DISK EXTENT.  THE CORE IMAGE DIRECTORY ALWAYS    C1R03470

                                    940 *********************************************************************** C1R09520
                                    941 *                                                                       C1R09530
                                    942 * THE SOURCE 2311 SYSRES USED FOR THIS PROGRAM INCLUDES A CORE IMAGE    C1R09540
                                    943 * LIBRARY (ALREADY COPIED) AND A RELOCATABLE LIBRARY (TO BE COPIED      C1R09550
                                    944 * IN THS SECTION).                                                      C1R09560
                                    945 *                                                                       C1R09570
                                    946 * COPY THE RELOCATABLE LIBRARY.  THIS IS MUCH SIMPLER THAN COPYING      C1R09580
                                    947 * THE CORE IMAGE LIBRARY BECAUSE THE DIRECTORY AND LIBRARY BLOCK SIZES  C1R09590
                                    948 * ARE THE SAME ON 2311 AND 2314.                                        C1R09600
                                    949 *                                                                       C1R09610
                                    950 * BUT THE DIRECTORY IS A TEENY BIT MORE DIFFICULT BECAUSE THE FIRST 80  C1R09620
                                    951 * BYTES OF THE FIRST DIRECTORY RECORD (EQUAL TO FIVE ENTRIES) IS USED   C1R09630
                                    952 * FOR THE DIRECTORY CONTROL RECORD.                                     C1R09640
                                    953 *                                                                       C1R09650
                                    954 * BECAUSE BLOCK SIZES ARE THE SAME FOR DIR AND LIBRARY, WE'LL JUST      C1R09660
                                    955 * COPY THE DIRECTORY AND THE LIBRARY BLOCK FOR BLOCK FROM THE 2311      C1R09670
                                    956 * VOLUME TO THE 2314 VOLUME.  WHILE PROCESSING THE DIRECTORY, WE'LL     C1R09680
                                    957 * RECALCULATE THE BBCCHHR FROM 2311 TO 2314 BY CONVERTING IT TO A       C1R09690
                                    958 * RELATIVE BLOCK ADDRESS FROM THE START OF THE LIBRARY AND THEN         C1R09700
                                    959 * CONVERTING THAT BACK TO THE CORRECT BBCCHHR TO 2314 TRACK GEOMETRY    C1R09710
                                    960 *                                                                       C1R09720
                                    961 * A SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY WILL ALSO BE COPIED, BUT THAT LIBRARY      C1R09730
                                    962 * WILL COME FROM ANOTHER SYSRES.  THE SAME DIRECTORY TRANSLATION WILL   C1R09740
                                    963 * BE DONE.                                                              C1R09750
                                    964 *                                                                       C1R09760
                                    965 *********************************************************************** C1R09770



                                    967 *********************************************************************** C1R09790
                                    968 * READ 2311 RELOCATABLE DIRECTORY (RLD) AND SET UP TO CREATE 2314       C1R09800
                                    969 *      DIRECTORY.                                                       C1R09810
                                    970 *                                                                       C1R09820
                                    971 *   RLD STARTS AT THE ADDRESS POINTED TO BY C0H1R2 ON 2311.  THE        C1R09830
                                    972 *   ADDRESS WAS SAVED DURING DURING THE TRANSFER OF C0H1 FROM 2311      C1R09840
                                    973 *   TO 2314.                                                            C1R09850
                                    974 *                                                                       C1R09860
                                    975 *   THE NEW RLD IS LOCATED AT THE 2314 C0H1R2, BUT WE CAN JUST USE      C1R09870
                                    976 *   THE RELOCATABLE LIBRARY STATUS RECORD TO LOCATE THINGS.             C1R09880
                                    977 *                                                                       C1R09890
                                    978 *   AS DIRECTORY RECORDS ARE COPIED, THE ENTRIES ARE ALTERED TO         C1R09900
                                    979 *   UPDATE THE CHR USING 2314 TRACK GEOMETRY.  THE 2311 CHR IS          C1R09910
                                    980 *   CONVERTED TO A BLOCK ADDRESS RELATIVE TO THE START OF THE 2311      C1R09920
                                    981 *   LIBRARY AND THEN CONVERTED BACK TO A 2314 CCHHRR.                   C1R09930
                                    982 *                                                                       C1R09940
                                    983 *   REGISTER USAGE:                                                     C1R09950
                                    984 *      R6 - COUNT OF 2314 DIR ENTRIES LEFT IN CURRENT DIR RECORD        C1R09960
                                    985 *      R7 - POINTER TO CURRENT 2314 DIRECTORY RECORD                    C1R09970
                                    986 *      R8 - COUNT OF 2311 DIR ENTRIES LEFT IN CURRENT DIR RECORD        C1R09980
                                    987 *      R9 - POINTER TO CURRENT 2311 DIRECTORY RECORD                    C1R09990
                                    988 *                                                                       C1R10000

                                   1267 *********************************************************************** C1R12790
                                   1268 *                                                                       C1R12800
                                   1269 * THE SOURCE 2311 SYSRES USED FOR THIS PROGRAM INCLUDES A CORE IMAGE    C1R12810
                                   1270 * LIBRARY AND A RELOCATABLE LIBRARY (ALREADY COPIED).  A SECOND SYSRES  C1R12820
                                   1271 * INCLUDES A SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY THAT MUST BE COPIED TO THE        C1R12830
                                   1272 * TARGET 2314 SYSRES.                                                   C1R12840
                                   1273 *                                                                       C1R12850
                                   1274 * COPY THE SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY.  THIS IS MUCH THE SAME AS THE      C1R12860
                                   1275 * RELOCATABLE LIBRARY, AND AS WITH THE RELOCATABLE LIBRARY, THE         C1R12870
                                   1276 * DIRECTORY AND LIBRARY BLOCK SIZES ARE THE SAME ON 2311 AND 2314.      C1R12880
                                   1277 *                                                                       C1R12890
                                   1278 * AND THE DIRECTORY IS A TEENY BIT MORE DIFFICULT BECAUSE THE FIRST 80  C1R12900
                                   1279 * BYTES OF THE FIRST DIRECTORY RECORD (EQUAL TO FIVE ENTRIES) IS USED   C1R12910
                                   1280 * FOR THE DIRECTORY CONTROL RECORD.                                     C1R12920
                                   1281 *                                                                       C1R12930
                                   1282 * BECAUSE BLOCK SIZES ARE THE SAME FOR DIR AND LIBRARY, WE'LL JUST      C1R12940
                                   1283 * COPY THE DIRECTORY AND THE LIBRARY BLOCK FOR BLOCK FROM THE 2311      C1R12950
                                   1284 * VOLUME TO THE 2314 VOLUME.  WHILE PROCESSING THE DIRECTORY, WE'LL     C1R12960
                                   1285 * RECALCULATE THE BBCCHHR FROM 2311 TO 2314 BY CONVERTING IT TO A       C1R12970
                                   1286 * RELATIVE BLOCK ADDRESS FROM THE START OF THE LIBRARY AND THEN         C1R12980
                                   1287 * CONVERTING THAT BACK TO THE CORRECT BBCCHHR TO 2314 TRACK GEOMETRY    C1R12990
                                   1288 *                                                                       C1R13000
                                   1289 * THIS SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY COMES FROM ANOTHER SYSRES VOLUME,       C1R13010
                                   1290 * NOT THE SAME ONE THAT THE RELO AND CORE IMAGE LIBRARIES CAME FROM,    C1R13020
                                   1291 * BUT IT IS PART OF THE SAME DISTRIBUTION TAPE.                         C1R13030
                                   1292 *                                                                       C1R13040
                                   1293 *********************************************************************** C1R13050



                                   1295 *********************************************************************** C1R13070
                                   1296 * READ 2311 SOURCE STATEMENT DIRECTORY (SLD) AND SET UP TO CREATE 2314  C1R13080
                                   1297 *      DIRECTORY.                                                       C1R13090
                                   1298 *                                                                       C1R13100
                                   1299 *   SLD STARTS AT THE ADDRESS POINTED TO BY C0H1R3 ON SLB2311.  THE     C1R13110
                                   1300 *   ADDRESS WAS SAVED DURING INITIALIZATION OF THIS PROGRAM             C1R13120
                                   1301 *                                                                       C1R13130
                                   1302 *   THE NEW SLD IS POINTED TO BY 2314 C0H1R2, BUT WE CAN JUST USE       C1R13140
                                   1303 *   THE SOURCE STATEMENT LIBRARY STATUS RECORD TO LOCATE THINGS.        C1R13150
                                   1304 *                                                                       C1R13160
                                   1305 *   AS DIRECTORY ENTRIES ARE COPIED, THEY ARE ALTERED TO UPDATE THE     C1R13170
                                   1306 *   CHR USING 2314 TRACK GEOMETRY.  THE 2311 CHR IS CONVERTED TO A      C1R13180
                                   1307 *   BLOCK ADDRESS RELATIVE TO THE START OF THE 2311 LIBRARY AND THEN    C1R13190
                                   1308 *   CONVERTED BACK TO A 2314 CCHHRR.                                    C1R13200
                                   1309 *                                                                       C1R13210
                                   1310 *   REGISTER USAGE:                                                     C1R13220
                                   1311 *      R6 - COUNT OF 2314 DIR ENTRIES LEFT IN CURRENT DIR RECORD        C1R13230
                                   1312 *      R7 - POINTER TO CURRENT 2314 DIRECTORY RECORD                    C1R13240
                                   1313 *      R8 - COUNT OF 2311 DIR ENTRIES LEFT IN CURRENT DIR RECORD        C1R13250
                                   1314 *      R9 - POINTER TO CURRENT 2311 DIRECTORY RECORD                    C1R13260
                                   1315 *                                                                       C1R13270

                                   1740 * INITIALIZE AN AREA OF STORAGE.  THE FIRST BYTE OF THE AREA HAS BEEN   C1R17410
                                   1741 * SET BY THE CALLER TO THE VALUE TO BE USED TO CLEAR THE REST OF THE    C1R17420
                                   1742 * AREA.                                                                 C1R17430

                                   1801 *                                                                       C1R18020
                                   1802 * EXECUTE 2314 CHANNEL PROGRAM AND WAIT FOR COMPLETION.  NO ERROR       C1R18030
                                   1803 * HANDLING AS THIS PROGRAM RUNS IN AN EMULATION ENVIRONMENT.            C1R18040
                                   1804 *                                                                       C1R18050
                                   1805 * ENTRY POINTS                                                          C1R18060
                                   1806 *    XIO - USED FOR READS AND DATA-ONLY (NON-FORMATTING WRITES)         C1R18070
                                   1807 *    XIOFW - USED FOR FORMATTING WRITES OF A SINGLE RECORD.  THIS       C1R18080
                                   1808 *       ROUTINE WILL CONSTRUCT A COUNT FIELD AT THE START OF THE I/O    C1R18090
                                   1809 *       AREA FROM CCW INFORMATION AND THE SEARCH FIELD POINTED TO       C1R18100
                                   1810 *       BY R1.  COUNT FIELD KEYLEN ALWAYS SET TO ZERO FOR THIS.         C1R18110
                                   1811 *                                                                       C1R18120
                                   1812 * AT ENTRY:                                                             C1R18130
                                   1813 *    R1 POINTS AT THE OPERATION'S CURSOR, WHICH INCLUDES THE            C1R18140
                                   1814 *         SEEK/SEARCH BBCCHHR ID AND THE ADDRESS OF THE DTFPH TO BE     C1R18150
                                   1815 *         USED                                                          C1R18160
                                   1816 *    R15 POINTS AT THE CALLER'S CCW(S).  THESE CCWS LOGICALLY FOLLOW    C1R18170
                                   1817 *        THE SEEK/SEARCH/TIC NEEDED TO LOCATE CYL/HEAD/REC FOR THE      C1R18180
                                   1818 *        OPERATION REQUESTED BY THE CALLER                              C1R18190
                                   1819 *    DATA AREA POINTED TO BY ANY/ALL CCWS SET AS NEEDED                 C1R18200
                                   1820 *                                                                       C1R18210
                                   1821 * NOTE:                                                                 C1R18220
                                   1822 *    FOR FORMATTING WRITE OPERATIONS WHEN WRITING MULTIPLE RECORDS      C1R18230
                                   1823 *    (COMMAND-CHAINING FORMATTING WRITE CCW'S), CALLER IS EXPECTED      C1R18240
                                   1824 *    TO PROVIDE COUNT FIELDS AND SHOULD USE THE XIO ENTRY POINT.        C1R18250
                                   1825 *                                                                       C1R18260
                                   1826 * REGISTER USAGE:                                                       C1R18270
                                   1827 *    R0  = WORK REGISTER, NOT SAVED NOR RESTORED (XIOFW ENTRY ONLY)     C1R18280

                                   1830 *    R14 = WORK REGISTER, NOT SAVED NOR RESTORED (XIOFW ENTRY ONLY)     C1R18310

                                   1832 *                                                                       C1R18330

                                   1885 *                                                                       C1R18800

                                   1947 *********************************************************************** C1R19420
                                   1948 *                                                                       C1R19430
                                   1949 * TRANSLATE A 2311 BBCCHHR TO THE EQUIVALENT LOCATION ON A 2314.        C1R19440
                                   1950 *                                                                       C1R19450
                                   1951 * THIS ROUTINE DOES A TWO-STEP TRANSLATION.  FIRST, THE 2311 BBCCHHR    C1R19460
                                   1952 * IS CONVERTED TO A BLOCK NUMBER RELATIVE TO THE START OF THE LIBRARY   C1R19470
                                   1953 * OR DIRECTORY THAT CONTAINS THE BBCCHHR.  SECOND, THE ROUTINE          C1R19480
                                   1954 * CONVERTS THE BLOCK NUMBER BACK TO AN ABSOLUTE BBCCHHR ON A 2314.      C1R19490
                                   1955 *                                                                       C1R19500
                                   1956 * THE INPUT CURSOR PROVIDES THE DEVICE TRACK GEOMETRY, RECORDS PER      C1R19510
                                   1957 * TRACK, AND DIRECTORY OR LIBRARY ABSOLUTE STARTING TRACK FOR THE       C1R19520
                                   1958 * INPUT BBCCHHR.  THE OUTPUT CURSOR PROVIDES THE SAME INFORMATION FOR   C1R19530
                                   1959 * THE TARGET 2314 LIBRARY OR DIRECTORY.  USE OF CURSOR DATA ELIMINATES  C1R19540
                                   1960 * ANY NEED FOR THIS ROUTINE TO KNOW WHAT KIND OF LIBRARY OR DIRECTORY   C1R19550
                                   1961 * IS BEING PROCESSED.                                                   C1R19560
                                   1962 *                                                                       C1R19570
                                   1963 * AT ENTRY:                                                             C1R19580
                                   1964 *    FIELD WORKBCHR CONTAINS THE INPUT BBCCHHR                          C1R19590
                                   1965 *    R0 POINTS TO THE OUTPUT CURSOR                                     C1R19600
